# Title:Point Source catalogue on WMAP 7-year data
# Authors:Scodeller, Hansen and Marinucci, arxiv:xxxx.xxxx
#
#Description
#---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Column    Units    Explanantion
#
#  1        -        Source Number
#  2        deg      Right ascension (J2000)
#  3        deg      Declination (J2000)
#  4,5      deg      Galactic longitude(4) and latitude (5)
#  6,7      Jy       Flux and error in K-band
#  8,9      Jy       Flux and error in Ka-band
#  10,11    Jy       Flux and error in Q-band
#  12,13    Jy       Flux and error in V-band
#  14,15    Jy       Flux and error in W-band
#  16       -        5 detection specification flags, "C" if 5sigma in given channel, "F" if 5sigma in internal template and 3sigma in given channel and "." if not found in given channel
#  17       -        3 identification flags with catalogues at similar frequencies with identification radius 15 arcmin, "W" for identification with WMAP-7year-catalogues, "N" for identification 
#                      with the NEWPS_5yr_5s-catalogue, "P" for the PLANCK-ERCSC (at 30, 44, 70, 100 GHz only); "." if not identified in a given catalogue
#  18       -        Lower frequency catalogues (GB6,PMN,NVSS,SUMSS) identification (identification radius 15'), "..." means no identification
#  19       arcmin   Distance to the lower frequency counterpart
#  20       -        2 lower frequency identification flags, "M" for multiple possible identification (the brightest one is listed), "A" if the counterpart has a flux of less than 0.1 Jy
#  21       -        5 flags for bias correction specification, "I" if the bias correction has been done via the internal templates in the given channel, "." if done with the standard approach. 
#---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
